 iske tahat ek hi parivaar ke do logon ko chunaav ladane kii anumati nahin di jaaegi

 ' He said, 'change of seat will be allowed only in case of 34 reserved seats
 saath hi ek parivaar, ek tikat kaa faisla antim hoga, ise nahin badla jayega

 hamale main 30 log maare gaye or kai anya ghayal ho gaye
 Authorized sources said on Sunday that the Union Home Ministry has summoned a detailed report from the Chhattisgarh government on the incident

 This is the largest Naxalite attack in Central India after 6 April 2010
 naksaliyon ne us samay dantewada jile main hamalaa kar kendriya rigerv police bal (siarpief) or rajya police ke kareeb 75 surakshakarmiyon kii hatya kar di thi

 chikangunia bahut teji se fail rahaa he
 Chikungunya is an infectious disease spread by Aedes mosquito
 is beemaari ke lakshan machhar kaatane ke turant baad najar nahin aate hai
 The infection starts two to three days after the mosquito bites
 chiknugania jaanaleva nahin he lekin agar samay rahete iskaa ilaaj nahin kiya jaae to ye khatarnaak sabit ho saktaa he
 In such a situation, start treatment as soon as its symptoms are seen so that the danger associated with it can be avoided
 chikangunia ke lakshan:1
 The most prominent symptom of chikungunya is that it causes severe joint pain
 bukhaar hone se pehle sharir main tej dard hota he
 Sometimes the pain is so much that it is difficult for Kimeries to get up from the bed
 2
 Chikungunya causes high fever
 kabhi-kabhi taapmaana 104 degree tak bhi pahunch jaataa he
 It is also cold with fever
 3
 Chikungunya causes rash on the body within 3 to 4 days after fever
 4
 Vomiting, headache and muscle strain are the main symptoms of this disease
 5
 Many times the eyes turn red and water starts coming
 chikangunia main khushki keeshikayat bhi ho jaati he
 Prevention measures from Chikungunya 1
 apane aas-paas kahin bhi pani jamaa nahin hone den
 Mosquitoes thrive in stagnant water
 khud ko machharon se bachaana bahut jaruri he
 Use mosquito nets at bedtime
 2
 Wear full clothes
 sharir ko dhakkar rakhen taaki machharon se bache rahen
 3
 ghar ko saaf-suthra rakhen
 Clean the place outside the house, in pots, garden, or at any place where water can accumulate
 jahaan sillen ho vahaan chooney kaa chhidkaav karen
 4
 kitnashkon kaa chhidkaav karen jisase machhar naa punap saken
 The treatment of chikungunya is true that no chikungunya vaccine is available yet
 aise main bukhaar or jodon ke dard ko kam karne ke liye doctor paracetamol lene kii salaah dete hai
 During this time, relax as much as possible and stay in touch with your doctor
 aaj desh or duniya main kya kuch hua khaas jaanane ke liye yahaan padhein dinabhar kii badi khabaren ekasaath
